3305
3306#ifndef __G_CONSTRUCTOR_H__
3307#define __G_CONSTRUCTOR_H__
3308
3309/*
3310 If G_HAS_CONSTRUCTORS is true then the compiler support *both* constructors and
3311 destructors, in a usable way, including e.g. on library unload. If not you're on
3312 your own.
3313
3314 Some compilers need #pragma to handle this, which does not work with macros,
3315 so the way you need to use this is (for constructors):
3316
3317 #ifdef G_DEFINE_CONSTRUCTOR_NEEDS_PRAGMA
3318 #pragma G_DEFINE_CONSTRUCTOR_PRAGMA_ARGS(my_constructor)
3319 #endif
3320 G_DEFINE_CONSTRUCTOR(my_constructor)
3321 static void my_constructor(void) {
3322 ...
3323 }
3324
3325*/
3326
3327#ifndef __GTK_DOC_IGNORE__
3328
3329#if __GNUC__ > 2 || (__GNUC__ == 2 && __GNUC_MINOR__ >= 7)
3330
3331#define G_HAS_CONSTRUCTORS 1
3332
3333#define G_DEFINE_CONSTRUCTOR(_func) static void __attribute__((constructor)) _func (void);
3334#define G_DEFINE_DESTRUCTOR(_func) static void __attribute__((destructor)) _func (void);
3335
3336#elif defined (_MSC_VER)
3337
3338/*
3339 * Only try to include gslist.h if not already included via glib.h,
3340 * so that items using gconstructor.h outside of GLib (such as
3341 * GResources) continue to build properly.
3342 */
3343#ifndef __G_LIB_H__
3344#include "gslist.h"
3345#endif
3346
3347#include <stdlib.h>
3348
3349#define G_HAS_CONSTRUCTORS 1
3350
3351/* We do some weird things to avoid the constructors being optimized
3352 * away on VS2015 if WholeProgramOptimization is enabled. First we
3353 * make a reference to the array from the wrapper to make sure its
3354 * references. Then we use a pragma to make sure the wrapper function
3355 * symbol is always included at the link stage. Also, the symbols
3356 * need to be extern (but not dllexport), even though they are not
3357 * really used from another object file.
3358 */
3359
3360/* We need to account for differences between the mangling of symbols
3361 * for x86 and x64/ARM/ARM64 programs, as symbols on x86 are prefixed
3362 * with an underscore but symbols on x64/ARM/ARM64 are not.
3363 */
3364#ifdef _M_IX86
3365#define G_MSVC_SYMBOL_PREFIX "_"
3366#else
3367#define G_MSVC_SYMBOL_PREFIX ""
3368#endif
3369
3370#define G_DEFINE_CONSTRUCTOR(_func) G_MSVC_CTOR (_func, G_MSVC_SYMBOL_PREFIX)
3371#define G_DEFINE_DESTRUCTOR(_func) G_MSVC_DTOR (_func, G_MSVC_SYMBOL_PREFIX)
3372
3373#define G_MSVC_CTOR(_func,_sym_prefix) \
3374 static void _func(void); \
3375 extern int (* _array ## _func)(void); \
3376 int _func ## _wrapper(void); \
3377 int _func ## _wrapper(void) { _func(); g_slist_find (NULL, _array ## _func); return 0; } \
3378 __pragma(comment(linker,"/include:" _sym_prefix # _func "_wrapper")) \
3379 __pragma(section(".CRT$XCU",read)) \
3380 __declspec(allocate(".CRT$XCU")) int (* _array ## _func)(void) = _func ## _wrapper;
3381
3382#define G_MSVC_DTOR(_func,_sym_prefix) \
3383 static void _func(void); \
3384 extern int (* _array ## _func)(void); \
3385 int _func ## _constructor(void); \
3386 int _func ## _constructor(void) { atexit (_func); g_slist_find (NULL, _array ## _func); return 0; } \
3387 __pragma(comment(linker,"/include:" _sym_prefix # _func "_constructor")) \
3388 __pragma(section(".CRT$XCU",read)) \
3389 __declspec(allocate(".CRT$XCU")) int (* _array ## _func)(void) = _func ## _constructor;
3390
